<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Syncs with <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code> state of fieldset</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Syncs with form <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">reset</code> events</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Can programmatically set radio group value</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Can programmatically focus and blur radio items</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To set up the radio group correctly, you&#x27;ll need to understand its anatomy and
how we name its parts.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the radio group package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> radio</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/radio-group&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The radio package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:radio-group/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" <h3 id="disabling-the-radio-group" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling the radio group<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-the-radio-group"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to disable all radio items.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>radio<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">disabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-the-initial-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> property to set the radio group&#x27;s initial value.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>radio<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;apple&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> to control selection externally.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>radio<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  value<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the radio group value changes, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> callback is invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>radio<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string | null }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;radio value is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="usage-within-forms" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within forms<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-forms"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To use radio group in forms, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>radio<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;fruits&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code> if the radio inputs should submit with a form outside the current DOM
subtree.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>radio<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;fruits&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">form</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;checkout-form&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="vertical-orientation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Vertical orientation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#vertical-orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code> when you need a vertical layout.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>radio<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="read-only-and-required-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Read-only and required state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#read-only-and-required-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">readOnly</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">required</code> to control form behavior.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>radio<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">readOnly</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">required</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="invalid-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Invalid state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#invalid-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code> to style and expose invalid form state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>radio<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">invalid</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each radio part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="checked-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Checked State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#checked-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the radio input is checked, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> attribute is added to the
item, control, and label parts.</p>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;radio-control&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;checked|unchecked&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<p>When the radio input is focused, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-focus</code> attribute is added to the

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The radio group machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; label: string; indicator: string; item: (value: string) =&gt; string; itemLabel: (value: string) =&gt; string; itemControl: (value: string) =&gt; string; itemHiddenInput: (value: string) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the radio. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The controlled value of the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The initial value of the checked radio when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the value of the radio group.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The name of the input fields in the radio
(Useful for form submission).</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">If `true`, the radio group will be disabled</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">If `true`, the radio group is marked as invalid.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">required</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">If `true`, the radio group is marked as required.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the radio group is read-only</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap <h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The radio group <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The current value of the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to set the value of the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clearValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to clear the value of the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">focus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to focus the radio group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getItemState</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(props: ItemProps) =&gt; ItemState</code><span class="d_block">Returns the state details of a radio input</span></li></ul>
<h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Adheres to the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/radiobutton" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">Radio Group WAI-ARIA design pattern</a></p>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Tab</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to either the checked radio item or the first radio item in the group.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Space</kbd></div><div>When focus is on an unchecked radio item, checks it.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowDown</kbd></div><div>Moves focus and checks the next radio item in the group.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowRight</kbd></div><div>Moves focus and checks the next radio item in the group.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowUp</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to the previous radio item in the group.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowLeft</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to the previous radio item in the group.</div></li></ul><a set.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/radio-group\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Radio\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Syncs with `disabled` state of fieldset\n- Syncs with form `reset` events\n- Can programmatically set radio group value\n- Can programmatically focus and blur radio items\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the radio package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"radio-group/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nTo set up the radio group correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"radio-group\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the radio group package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as radio from \"@zag-js/radio-group\"\n```\n\nThe radio package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"radio-group/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Disabling the radio group\n\nSet `disabled` to `true` to disable all radio items.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  disabled: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Setting the initial value\n\nUse the `defaultValue` property to set the radio group's initial value.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  defaultValue: \"apple\",\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled value\n\nUse `value` and `onValueChange` to control selection externally.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  value,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    setValue(details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for changes\n\nWhen the radio group value changes, the `onValueChange` callback is invoked.\n\n```jsx {2-7}\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string | null }\n    console.log(\"radio value is:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Usage within forms\n\nTo use radio group in forms, set `name`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  name: \"fruits\",\n})\n```\n\nSet `form` if the radio inputs should submit with a form outside the current DOM\nsubtree.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  name: \"fruits\",\n  form: \"checkout-form\",\n})\n```\n\n### Vertical orientation\n\nSet `orientation` when you need a vertical layout.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  orientation: \"vertical\",\n})\n```\n\n### Read-only and required state\n\nUse `readOnly` and `required` to control form behavior.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  readOnly: true,\n  required: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Invalid state\n\nSet `invalid` to style and expose invalid form state.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(radio.machine, {\n  invalid: true,\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach radio part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Checked State\n\nWhen the radio input is checked, the `data-state` attribute is added to the\nitem, control, and label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"radio\"][data-state=\"checked|unchecked\"] {\n  /* styles for radio checked or unchecked state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-control\"][data-state=\"checked|unchecked\"] {\n  /* styles for radio checked or unchecked state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-label\"][data-state=\"checked|unchecked\"] {\n  /* styles for radio checked or unchecked state */\n}\n```\n\n### Focused State\n\nWhen the radio input is focused, the `data-focus` attribute is added to the\nroot, control and label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"radio\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for radio focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-control\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for radio control focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-label\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for radio label focus state */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled State\n\nWhen the radio is disabled, the `data-disabled` attribute is added to the root,\ncontrol and label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"radio\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for radio disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-control\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for radio control disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for radio label disabled state */\n}\n```\n\n### Invalid State\n\nWhen the radio is invalid, the `data-invalid` attribute is added to the root,\ncontrol and label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"radio\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for radio invalid state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-control\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for radio control invalid state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"radio-label\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for radio label invalid state */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe radio group machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"radio-group\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe radio group `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"radio-group\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\nAdheres to the\n[Radio Group WAI-ARIA design pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/radiobutton)\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"radio-group\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Radio Group\",\"description\":\"Using the radio group machine in your
